Red Bandits Invade Eastern Hubei 133

Wuxue's Situation Extremely Critical

The Bandits in Tianmen and Qianjiang Have Been Heavily Defeated

Following the Fall of Guangji, Huangmei and Wuxue are in Extreme Danger

A Hankou dispatch reports that the military suppression of bandits in Hubei Province has recently become extremely tense. In the central Hubei area, the largest concentration of bandits is in the area of HuahLiu River near Zaoshi in Tianmen County. The 48th Division of the 10th Army, along with Zhang Zhenhan's 41st Division and Xiao Zhichu's 44th Division, jointly surrounded and suppressed them. After seven days and nights of bloody battle, no less than 17,000 bandits were killed. It is also rumored that the bandit leader, Duan Dechang, was wounded and killed in this battle. As for the suppression of the He bandits' lair in Qianjiang, it is being carried out by the Sichuan Army, with Wang Lingji in command. They have divided into four routes to advance. The first route, under Guo Xun, engaged in fierce fighting with the bandits at Zhoujiaji. The second route, under Commander Zhang, engaged in fierce fighting with He Long himself at Xia Banghu. The third route, under Commander Fan, engaged in fierce fighting with the bandits at Longwan. The fourth route, under Commander Tong, engaged in fierce fighting with the bandits at Chentuokou. The fighting in the Xia Banghu area was particularly fierce. On the 13th, this office received a telegram from Guo Xun, stating that since the 7th, he had been fighting with He Duan in the Guankou, Meijialing, and Zhaojiatai areas southwest of Qianjiang, fighting hard until the evening of the 11th before defeating the bandits. They immediately occupied Qianjiang County. The bandit forces retreated toward Tuochuanbu and are currently being pursued. The bandits suffered extremely heavy losses this time, with casualties estimated at over 2,000, and so on. This telegram was sent from Qianjiang, so it should be reliable. However, the situation in eastern Hubei has suddenly become tense again. The counties in eastern Hubei are half connected to Henan and half bordering Anhui. Except for Huang'an, which is still in the hands of the bandits, the other counties are relatively peaceful. On the 13th, it was suddenly reported that the 25th Army, part of the Red Bandit's Fourth Front Army, claiming to have two divisions, had bypassed Yingshan via Ximaban in Qishui and were advancing on Huanggang. Guangji County fell on the 12th. Huangmei is in imminent danger. County Magistrate Gui Fu Cang is supervising the troops to defend the city while also telegraphing the Civil Affairs Department to request assistance from the Pacification Headquarters. However, it is said that the Red Bandits are very powerful and will not be satisfied with just taking Huanggang. Their slogan is to meet in Wuhan. Therefore, after the fall of Guangji, Wuxue, which belongs to the county, is also in a precarious situation. Wuxue is an important town in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River, and its preservation is essential for both military and transportation purposes. Representatives from the local chamber of commerce, Guo Renqiu, Xu Zhuozhai, Zhong Shaolian, and Ku Hantao, traveled day and night to Hankou. At 2:00 PM on the 13th, they went to the Pacification Headquarters to report. Because He Chengjun had gone to Lushan, the Chief of Staff, Yang Kuiyi, received them. The representatives reported that the Zhang Wanxin troops stationed in Wuxue were weak and in a very dangerous situation. They requested that capable troops be dispatched quickly to rescue them. Yang replied that there were sufficient preparations to suppress the bandits in eastern Hubei. The Du Brigade of the 47th Division, which arrived in Hankou on the 12th, has already gone to garrison the area to assist in the suppression as the opportunity arises. The entire unit has arrived, and more troops will continue to arrive in the coming days. The defense of the river surface will be handled by Zeng Yiding, commander of the Second Fleet stationed in Hankou, who will dispatch the Yongsheng warship to suppress the situation. The defense of Wuxue will be further consolidated, and so on. The representatives were satisfied with the results and left. That evening, the Pacification Headquarters received a telegram from Dong Jianbo, regimental commander of the 34th Division in Wuxue, stating that two regiments of Shangguan Yunxiang's troops had arrived, and the people's hearts were stable. According to some sources, Shangguan himself has decided to go to Wuxue on the 14th to direct and supervise the suppression. The division sent to Hankou this time is the First Brigade, the Second Brigade, and the division headquarters personnel, who are continuing to travel west from Nanjing and are expected to arrive completely around the 15th. After that, they will be stationed in Wuxue. In addition, the 54th Division, under Hao Mengling, will also leave Jiangxi for Hubei to garrison eastern Hubei and assist in the suppression. Although the bandits are brave, they will not be able to do anything.

The Pacification Headquarters, in its eagerness to suppress the bandits this time, is anxious to rectify military discipline and win over the people's hearts. On the 7th, it received a telegram from Chiang Kai-shek, relaying instructions to all armies regarding the policy of not punishing those who were coerced into joining the bandits in the recovered areas. On the 8th, it ordered all armies to rectify military discipline, focus on practical education, and assist the people in self-defense. Furthermore, in the past, the army had raised funds locally, with many names and nothing but exactions. The people were greatly distressed, and the army could not support itself. At this time of tense bandit suppression, this should be taken as a profound warning. On the 12th, it also issued separate instructions to the bandit suppression units to strictly prohibit this practice. (June 13th)

The 19th Route Army

The First Batch Arrives in Quanzhou

The Fuzhou Pacification Headquarters is Being Organized

The Red Bandits Flee from Longyan Again

A Fuzhou dispatch reports that the first batch of the 19th Route Army, which came from Jiangsu to Fujian to suppress bandits, Mao Weishou's division, totaling over 12,000 men, arrived in Quanzhou on the 7th, 8th, and 9th, disembarking from Xiutu Port and garrisoning inside and outside Quanzhou City. Merchants and civilians along the way set off firecrackers to express their welcome. The ships continued to go to Zhenjiang to load the second batch, Qu Shounian's division, to Fujian. It is reported that the army temporarily plans to garrison in Tong'an, Haicheng, Jinjiang, and other counties, and will be redeployed after Commander Cai Tingkai arrives. However, the people of Zhangzhou are very eager for the army to enter Zhangzhou as soon as possible because they distrust Zhang Zhen's division. On the 11th, the provincial government specially appointed Commissioner Lin Zhiyuan as the Special Commissioner for Post-War Affairs in Zhangzhou to go to Zhangzhou to assist Zhang Zhen in receiving the 19th Route Army and to observe the situation. If Zhang Zhen's position is indeed difficult, he will temporarily take over the 49th Division to await the central government's resolution. Furthermore, after Zhangzhou was recovered, various miscellaneous troops used the name of bandit suppression to set up their own banners and disturb the local area, which should also be dealt with as soon as possible to avoid harming the people.

As for the Fuzhou Pacification Headquarters, it is reported that Jiang Guangnai will first send Zhang Xiang to Fujian to organize it. After the Red Bandits withdrew from Zhangzhou to Longyan, it is reported that they have fled again. Before leaving, they shot 11 people in Longyan. Another group of over 500 people left for Nanyangba on the morning of the 3rd. Their destination is unknown. Only about 1,000 local Red bandits remain in Longyan City to guard it. Observing the bandits' movements, they will either flee back to Tinglian or harass Hangyong. The bandits in Longyan claimed that they were going to attack Dapu and enter the Dongjiang River. It is not known whether this is a feint or if they have other intentions. The bandits in the Kanshi area have not yet withdrawn. After the security teams searched and suppressed the areas near Shizhong, there were no traces of bandits, and local order has been restored. The traffic from Zhangzhou to Shizhong has also been restored. The security team has sent telephone soldiers to repair the telegraph wires along the Zhangzhou road, so Shizhong and Zhangzhou can now communicate. In addition, seven bandits who escaped from Longyan brought three Type 38 rifles, three Type 30 rifles, and one Russian-made Type 79 rifle to Shizhong and surrendered to the security team. According to them, life among the bandits is very difficult. Now that they hear they are returning to Jiangxi, many are unwilling to go, and many are escaping, and so on.

Zhejiang and Jiangxi Joint Suppression of Fang Bandits 134

Fang Zhizheng Suffers a Disastrous Defeat in a Fierce Attack on Shangrao

The Bandit Organizations in Geyuan Are All Bombed

A Nanchang dispatch reports that Fang Zhimin, the Red Bandit in eastern Jiangxi, is the chairman of the pseudo-Jiangbei Revolutionary Committee and the pseudo-Xinjiang Soviet. Since 1927, he has been active in Yiyang, Hengfeng, Guixi, Qianshan, Shangrao, Dexing, Fuliang, Leping, and Wannan. The Xinjiang and Raohe river basins have suffered immeasurably. Recently, this bandit led the pseudo-10th Army under Zhou Jianping to capture Hengfeng, and his power became even more rampant. A few days ago, he besieged Dexing for five days. Because the Li Division and Zhang Brigade firmly defended the city, he failed and retreated to his old lair in Hengfeng, but he still harassed the nearby counties, causing unspeakable suffering. He Yingqin then transferred Jiang Dingwen's troops from Zhejiang to advance towards Yushan, and Zhou Hunyuan's division advanced from Jinxi towards Guixi, joining the Li and Wang divisions originally stationed in eastern Jiangxi to encircle and suppress the Fang bandits. The Fang bandits were surrounded on all sides, so they again used the old trick of avoiding the strong and attacking the weak. Before the arrival of all the divisions, they used all their strength to pounce on Wang Jinwen's division, hoping to defeat the division, capture Shangrao, and join forces with Deng Qi, Huang Dao, and other bandits in Qianshan, preparing to retreat to Fujian (Qianshan borders Chong'an in Fujian). According to military reports from Hekou, about 20,000 Fang and Shao bandits are gathered in Hengfeng, with 3,000 rifles, machine guns, mortars, and artillery of all kinds. On the 6th of this month, they attacked Shangrao with all their forces, and the fire was extremely fierce. The reason for this is that since the bandits occupied Luojiaqiao and Yinjiafang, they cut off the telegraph and telephone lines from Shangrao to Hekou to cut off official communication and supplies. On the other hand, they divided into three sides from Longtan, Zhuxi Bridge, and other places to attack Raocheng. After receiving the warning, Division Commander Wang Jinwen, together with Brigade Commander Hua Musheng, personally led the Li and Wang regiments to meet the enemy in different directions. At the same time, he used radio to order the Hekou Division Headquarters to dispatch troops stationed in the area to advance to Liulukou to take a pincer attack. After the arrangements were made, the fighting began. The bandits advancing head-on from Heng to Rao fired their rifles and cannons, and their attack was very fierce. Wang's army calmly responded and did not move. The troops directly under the Division Headquarters, which bypassed the bandits' rear from Hekou, launched a fierce charge against the bandits. After five or six hours of fierce fighting, the bandits, because they were attacked from both sides, suffered heavy casualties and retreated to the Hengfeng border that night. But the bandits were still not discouraged and mobilized a large number of peasant bandits and rifle bandits to reinforce them. On the 7th and 8th, the counterattack became even more intense. On the morning of the 8th, Division Commander Wang changed his strategy because it was difficult to win from the front. He ordered the Li Regiment of the division to leave Longtan and Zhuxi Bridge, copy the bandits' right wing, and cooperate with the frontal encirclement and attack. At the same time, the air force team sent by the headquarters also soared in the sky and threw bombs at the dense ranks of the Fang bandits, killing many bandits. The bandits were forced by the planes and retreated to Gaokeng Shuangxikou in the northwest. The Li and Wang regiments took advantage of the victory and advanced more than 20 li deep into the Hengfeng border. In this battle, many bandits were killed and many guns, flags, and military supplies were seized. Division Commander Wang has already telegraphed a victory report yesterday. In addition to replying with praise, Minister He also ordered a thorough pursuit and suppression to achieve complete success. In addition, the Civil Affairs Department received a telegram from Peng Fusu, the magistrate of Qianshan County, stating that the Zou Qi bandits, a part of the Fang bandits, led more than 1,000 bandits with 500 to 600 guns to besiege the joint teams of the first and second districts of Xiangu Ridge in the county on the 26th of last month, attempting to seize their guns. The teams immediately came out to meet them. They were then reinforced by the teams from Longpao Mountain and other places, and they defeated the bandits. Later, the Huang Dao bandits on the south bank of the Qian River joined forces with the Zou bandits. The teams were weak and afraid that they were not their opponents, so they telegraphed the province for assistance. However, according to military sources, He Yingqin had already decided on a complete plan to suppress the Fang bandits in eastern Jiangxi. Zhou's division has arrived in Guixi, Jiang's division has arrived in Jiangxi from Zhejiang, and the Wang and Li divisions are also making arrangements and will begin the encirclement and suppression in a few days. Moreover, the aviation team bombed the bandits' bases in Hengfeng and Geyuan with dozens of heavy bombs one after another on Jiang Yu and other days, and all the pseudo-organizations were destroyed. According to a captured bandit from a certain division headquarters, the planes dropped bombs in Geyuan on the 7th and landed inside the pseudo-Northeast Soviet government, collapsing many houses, killing more than 20 important bandits, and injuring even more. The nearby arsenal was also bombed by the planes, and the surviving bandits fled like crows and beasts. (June 11th)

Suzhou 135

The 19th Army's Bandit Suppression Policy in Fujian: The 19th Army stationed in Suzhou was ordered to go to Fujian to suppress bandits. The 19th Headquarters is scheduled to leave Suzhou on the 20th. Commander Cai has left Suzhou for Shanghai to wait for the ships to go to Fujian. All circles here are preparing to hoist flags throughout the city to see them off when the headquarters leaves. The 87th Division of the 5th Army, which is coming to Suzhou to take over the defense, will open Suzhou to fill the defense immediately. All circles are also preparing to welcome them. It is reported that the 19th Army Headquarters has set a concrete policy for bandit suppression in Fujian: (1) Wipe out the Red Bandits, (2) Support people's self-defense as much as possible and promote local construction, (3) Comfort the homeless, (4) Eradicate opium, (5) Deploy national defense.

Water Patrol Seizes Five Bandits: Dai Mugen, the gang leader of the Shuihuobang, gathered crowds to harass the Shen Dian Bridge area of Xiangcheng. After someone reported this to the water patrol squadron, the police were dispatched to the Yuchunfa Teahouse in the town, arresting Zhang Yaosan, Wang Axing, Lu Zhaonian, Xu Fuxing, and the teahouse owner, Yu Chunfa. The gang leader, Dai Mugen, fled upon hearing the news and was not caught. Stolen goods such as clothing and silver jewelry were seized and taken back to Suzhou with the team, and sent to the Brigade Headquarters for review.

Wujiang 136

Xinsulu Steamer Robbed by Bandits: The Xinsulu steamer from Suzhou to Luxu was robbed by four bandits dressed in suits and Zhongshan suits, who were lying in ambush on the ship. When the ship arrived in Wujiang on the afternoon of yesterday (13th) at 1:00 PM, they pointed guns at the passengers and searched them near the Baodai Bridge. They stole silver dollars and jewelry worth over 1,000 yuan. After the robbery, they ordered the ship to stop on the shore and fled toward Suzhou.

Wuxi 137

Escaped Soldiers Surrounded and Arrested on the Bank of Qiugong: Near the Qiugong bank of the Nanshuang Temple in the 15th district of the county, a boat was moored at about 8:00 AM yesterday morning. There were six escaped soldiers in it, four with rifles and two unarmed. The villagers were suspicious and reported to the 1st squad of the 2nd squadron of the police brigade in the town. Special Agent Shi Fengqi led seven officers and five road protection soldiers to arrest them. However, when the escaped soldiers saw the police officers arriving, they first fled, and then took advantage of the terrain and opened fire to resist arrest. The police and soldiers also opened fire. After an hour of fierce fighting, the escaped soldiers were defeated and fled. One was shot and wounded and groaned in a pool of blood, and one was killed. The other four were also arrested. According to their confession, the wounded man was named Ma Zhonghua, and the other four were named Yang Chunhua, Li Guituan, Wu Yuemei, and Ye Shuting. They were all soldiers of the 9th company of the 54th Regiment of the 2nd Brigade of the 10th Division. When the troops were stationed in Jiaxing, Wu and Ye had asked for a month's leave and went to Wuxi with a friend from Qingshan Bay. Now that their leave was over, they planned to go to the 19th Route Army, but were arrested on the way, and so on. They were immediately sent to the city for strict interrogation.

Silk Factories Request Rent Reduction: Wuxi Chengfeng, Shengyu, Yingyi, Dafeng, Yeqin, Santai, Yuanyi, Defeng, Zhengyi, Yifeng, Yisheng, Yufeng, Yusheng, Housheng and other silk factories have been renting factories for business. Because of the years of failure and the national crisis, the silk factories have closed and production has stopped. The factory rent is unbearable, so yesterday they separately presented to the county government's Industrial Department, requesting instructions to the Chamber of Commerce, together with the Party Department, to convene factory owners and tenants to reduce or waive the rent as an example, to provide relief and alleviate the commercial difficulties.

Changshu 138

Large Number of Scattered Soldiers Arrive in the Countryside and Cause Trouble: Xianshengqiao Town, in the second district of the county, is an important town in the northeast countryside. On the morning of the 12th of this month, 32 people in military uniforms who looked like scattered soldiers suddenly came. They each carried a rifle. After arriving in the town, they bought kerosene and straw, saying that they wanted to burn down the entire town. At that time, residents and merchants were extremely panic and moved important items elsewhere. Then, the town chief, Chen Linxian, came forward to negotiate. The scattered soldiers demanded 1,000 silver dollars before they would leave. After repeated negotiations, they were given four silver dollars each. According to the soldiers, they were separated from the team and could not find it. They now intend to cross the river to Shanghai, and so on. At the same time, nearby residents reported this to the Zhenyu patrol ship anchored at Fukou. The ship immediately flew to Xianshengqiao to be on alert. Therefore, the scattered soldiers did not go north, but returned to Maojiaqiao with their weapons.

Nantong 139

Provincial Committee Comes to Nantong to Force Collection of House Tax: The provincial government believes that the house rent tax collected in Nantong is still less than 8,000 yuan, so it specially commissioned Huang Baipeng to come to Nantong to join with the county government to force the collection from house to house.

Sea Bandits Rampant in Daan Port: In the Daan Hong area at the junction of Tonghai, a large group of sea bandits has been operating recently. There are more than 40 bandit ships and more than 600 bandits. In addition to robbing on the river, because the fishing season has passed, fishermen are unwilling to buy fake flag licenses, so they threaten to burn their boats. In recent days, kidnapping cases have occurred frequently in nearby towns. The magistrates of Tonghai County have agreed to mobilize the water and land police teams to suppress them.

Funding Issues for the 25th Route Army: The 25th Route Army under Liang Guanying has a monthly salary of 200,000 yuan. In addition to a part allocated by the provincial government, the rest is borrowed from the counties north of the Yangtze River. Commander Liang has sent Senators Zhu and Han to Nantong to borrow 100,000 yuan from the Chamber of Commerce. The original letter said, "The funds for our army were originally issued by the central government on a monthly basis. However, due to the national crisis, the national treasury is empty, and the amount has been reduced repeatedly, and it is less than one-third of the original amount and cannot be issued as scheduled. The two thousand officers and soldiers of our army are in an unsustainable situation. Therefore, Senator Zhu Zeqing and Senator Han Shaoshi are specially sent to your association to borrow 100,000 yuan to maintain the emergency," and so on. This amount is currently being borrowed by the industrial and banking sectors for 20,000 yuan. The rest is being borrowed by the districts, but it is difficult to collect it all at once.

Yangzhou 140

Eighteen Merchant Guilds from Huai River Come to Yangzhou to Petition: On the matter of Wang Zhanghu, the Transport Envoy of the Lianghuai Salt District, coming to Yangzhou to improve the salt affairs on the four banks of Hubei, Hunan, western Anhui, and Anhui, the 18 merchant guilds from the Twelve Dike River ports believe that the change to transport by steamship affects the livelihoods of sailing merchants, so they organized a petition group of about 300 people and arrived in Yangzhou on the Pujin steamer on the morning of the 13th to petition Wang, the Transport Envoy, at the Sian Public Office. They were received by Representative Ye Yucang. The purpose of their petition was divided into three points: (1) Maintain sailing transport, (2) There is currently no shortage of sales on each bank, so there is no need for steamship transport, (3) The current living is extremely difficult, please urge the merchants to handle the transport. Representative Ye agreed to forward the petition to the director and then summoned the entire group. Representative Ye reported that the director had adopted the three points of the petition, but needed to submit a written document for forwarding to the Ministry of Finance, and gave them good advice and explained in detail the director's mission to Yangzhou, which was to reorganize the transport and sales plan. The petition points are part of the plan. The group was satisfied and dispersed.

Ningbo 141

The Massacre on Dengbu Island: Dengbu Mountain in Dinghai is a remote island where pirates come and go. The residents are all vigilant. In the past, the local residents organized a security team to protect themselves. Later, it was disbanded due to an incident and has been suspended for many years. Since the province ordered all counties to organize voluntary security teams, the Dinghai County government added two graduates from the training class, Jin Zheng and Gao Renfeng, to the mountain to establish a security team. Jin was weak in nature, and everything was controlled by Gao. Therefore, most of the recruited team members were bandits. They often relied on armed force to harass the villagers. Last month, a man named Fang from Jintang, who was working as a sailor on a foreign ship, smuggled four pistols from abroad and entrusted his cousin to sell them on the mountain. District Chief Xu Shouqing heard about this and ordered Captain Ren of the team to detain Fang and take him to the Daxao Temple, where he poured boiling water on his head and crushed him with a stone mill. When Fang was being tortured, an old woman surnamed Mou was chanting Buddha's name and witnessed the pitiful situation. She knelt on the ground and begged for mercy. Unexpectedly, the captain held a rattan stick, slammed it on the table, and scolded loudly. The old woman was frightened and became insane. She drowned herself in the river a few days later. Afterwards, all the residents of the mountain were indignant and jointly filed a lawsuit with the county with forty or fifty villagers. However, Ren had bad intentions. On the evening of the Dragon Boat Festival, he led Shang and others to Maoji Grocery Store with guns, shooting and killing the manager of the store, Hua Rong'an, and Hua Ade, one after another. Ren's heart was still not satisfied, and he searched through various homes. Four people were shot and injured for no reason, and eight were shot and killed. This is truly a terrible thing to hear.

Bandits Intimidate and Extort Unsuccessfully, Killing Two Children: The family of Chuan Yinsheng, a resident in front of the Gulou in Zhenhai, has more than 100 mu of good land and more than 10,000 yuan in cash, which has aroused the covetousness of bandits. On the 5th of this month, he received a threatening letter demanding 10,000 silver dollars, limited to an immediate response, otherwise, they would take extraordinary measures, and so on. Chuan had no choice but to negotiate for 100 yuan, but the bandits wanted at least 1,000 yuan. To avoid disaster, Chuan fled to Shanghai. However, at 12:00 PM that day, more than a dozen bandits suddenly came with guns and rushed in, searching everywhere for Chuan. They could not find him and took Chuan's two children, aged ten and six, out, intending to execute them. Seeing that the situation was not good, Chuan's wife begged repeatedly, willing to obey the order in full, but the bandits still did not listen and shot and killed the two children, fleeing towards the Xijiao Field.

Letter

Letter from the Lingbi County Government 142

To the Editors of Shenbao:

I recently read your special dispatch from Xuzhou in the issue of the 9th of this month, which contained a report about bandits from Lingbi robbing wheat from Xiao County. It said that the magistrate of Xiao County telegraphed the Anhui and Jiangsu provincial governments, stating that hundreds of bandits from Lingbi, armed with more than 200 guns, robbed hundreds of mu of wheat from the tenth district of Xiao County along the lake, and killed two civilians and injured five. Recently, they have even carried mortars and machine guns and carried out massacres, and so on. This is not true. The dispute between Lingbi and Xiao counties over the Qingzhong Lake fields has been going on for years. Every harvest season, the people of Xiao County crossed the border to forcibly cut and seize the wheat, resulting in armed fighting. In order to permanently resolve the dispute, a fundamental solution was proposed: abolish the fields and return them to the lake, and a telegram was sent to the Department of Civil Affairs of the provincial government to seek a proper solution. However, the people of Xiao County relied on force to carry out the invasion of the forbidden area. The people of Xiao County also did not comply with the orders and secretly planted every year, not only harvesting the wheat in the lake, but also further seizing the civilian fields in Lingbi County. In order to prevent this from happening, we repeatedly telegraphed the provincial governments of Anhui and Jiangsu and the Xiao County government to strictly prohibit it. We also sent training officers with teams to suppress and restrain the residents during the wheat season to prevent them from acting rashly. These were all on record. However, Wang Yirui and other civilians from Xiao County gathered more than 200 members of the Red Spear Society on the night of the 3rd of this month and secretly attacked the stationed police team at the Dawang Temple in Lingbi County, which is several miles away from the border of Xiao County. Although they broke through the encirclement, one soldier was still injured, and three rifles and one box gun were robbed, and many carts, cattle, and horses were looted from the Dawang Temple and other places. This was so rampant that it was almost like bandits. We telegraphed the provincial governments of Anhui and Jiangsu and the Xiao County government to strictly prohibit it in order to avoid expansion. According to subsequent reports, the people of Xiao County have increased their forces and launched a major attack, as if facing a major enemy. The situation is extremely precarious. We are now restraining our subordinates to avoid another major tragedy. This situation is obviously inconsistent with what was reported in your newspaper. We are hereby detailing the facts from beginning to end and requesting your newspaper to correct them in order to show credibility and maintain justice. This is our sincere prayer. Sincerely, Lingbi County Government, Anhui Province, June 11th.

Important News

Meeting of the Chinese Society for Social Education 143

Establishing the Status of Social Education by Improving the Academic System

Popularizing Education for the Masses Requires County-Level Organization

丨丨Mr. and Mrs. Niu Tiesheng Visit Wuxi to Attend 丨丨

(Wuxi Correspondence) The first session of the first board of directors of the Chinese Society for Social Education was held at 2:00 PM on the 11th at the Social Bridge Education College in this city. Attendees included Li Zheng, Yu Qingtang, Meng Xiancheng, Gao Yang, Zhao Mian, Shang Zhongyi, and Gan Yuyuan. Observers included Chen Li, Jiang Sunfang, Liu Yungu, Peng Baichuan, and more than ten others. Meng Xiancheng served as chairman, and Chen Dabai as secretary. The following resolutions were made: 1. Publish a monthly newsletter of the society's affairs. 2. Compile and print works on social education. 3. Prepare to establish a social education bookstore. 4. Continue to recruit members according to the regulations stipulated in the society's charter. 5. Add Liang Shuming, Zhuang Zexuan, and Dong Huaisan as directors of the society. 6. Draft an outline for the organizational structure of the society's board of directors' office, with one person elected from the standing directors to serve as director of the office. The original proposal was submitted to the directors for revision. 7. The term of office for the current board of directors and the postponement of the next board of directors election would be submitted to the annual meeting for discussion. 8. The annual meeting was scheduled to be held around August 20th in Hangzhou. The meeting then adjourned. At 10:00 AM on the 12th, the meeting continued at the Education College. Niu Tiesheng and his wife, Huang Meixian, also attended. Chaired by Li Zheng, the following resolutions were made: 1. Zhao Mian, Yu Qingtang, and Meng Xiancheng were elected as standing directors, and Gao Yang, Li Zheng, and Shang Zhongyi were elected as alternate standing directors. 2. Wuxi Education College was tentatively designated as the society's headquarters. 3. Shang Zhongyi, Lu Dianyang, Zheng Xiaocang, Hu Chengshu, Meng Xiancheng, Zhang Rentian, and Chen Xunzi were elected as a seven-member committee to prepare for the annual meeting, assisting the standing directors in handling security matters. 4. The society's work plan would be drafted by the standing directors. 5. The society's first annual budget was reviewed and approved, and the standing directors were instructed to revise and implement it based on actual circumstances. 6. The society's methods for receiving donations were drafted by Peng Baichuan, Zhong Lingxiu, and Gu Liangjie for review. 7. Regulations for members' correspondence and research were stipulated, allowing for mutual learning and improvement. The original proposer was asked to draft detailed regulations and submit them to the standing directors for review. 8. A second board of directors meeting would be convened one week before the annual meeting. 9. The society should propose that various provinces establish county-level units to conduct experiments in popularizing education for the masses. The original proposal was drafted by Gao Yang, Yu Qingtang, Zhao Mian, Chen Li, and Gan Yuyuan, and submitted to the Ministry of Education by the standing directors, along with separate letters to the education departments of various provincial and municipal governments, and notify members to find ways to promote its realization. 10. A proposal to improve China's academic system and establish the status of social education was drafted by Meng Xiancheng, Zhao Mian, Chen Li, Shang Zhongyi, and Yu Qingtang, and submitted to the next board of directors meeting for discussion. After the meeting, all the directors went to Taihu Hotel for dinner, hosted by the Wuxi directors. In the afternoon, they visited famous scenic spots such as Yuantouzhu, Xiaojishan, and Meiyuan. Mrs. Niu left Wuxi for Shanghai at 3:00 PM, and the directors from Hangzhou, Nanjing, and other places also left Wuxi that evening to return to their hometowns.

Municipal Education Bureau Orders Educational Institutions 146

To Participate in Native Cloth Exhibition

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued an order to municipal schools and social education institutions stating that, according to a letter from Zhang Ming, Director of the Shanghai County Farmers' Education Center, in order to make the Chinese people understand the advantages of native cloth and arouse their concept of loving native cloth, the first native cloth exhibition will be held from June 6th, with an opening ceremony on that day. On the 7th, the exhibition will still be held in Zhuanqiao. From the 8th, it will tour the entire county to promote production. On the 13th, 14th, and 15th, it will be publicly exhibited at the Penglai Market on Penglai Road in the Nanshi district of Shanghai. For the convenience of procurement, there will be an order department, and on the morning of the 15th, at 10:00 AM, a closing ceremony will be held. After the closing ceremony, a native cloth improvement association, a native cloth exhibition room, and a native cloth store will be organized to promote domestic products and practice thrift. However, this matter is significant and requires the support of everyone. Your Bureau is a leader in education in Shanghai, and a call from you will surely resonate throughout the valley. We hereby send this letter, respectfully requesting that you order all schools under your direct jurisdiction to promote this uniformly, etc., and attach a copy of the touring plan for the first native cloth exhibition. Accordingly, it has been ordered to promote domestic goods and implement this. The attached plan is hereby copied and issued, ordering all schools and social education institutions to promote this uniformly. This order.

Touring Plan for the First Native Cloth Exhibition of the Shanghai County Farmers' Education Center

1. Objective: To increase the effectiveness of the association. 2. Touring Locations and Dates: Minhang, June 8th and 9th; Maqiao, June 10th and 11th; Shanghai, June 13th, 14th, and 15th; Sanlin, June 16th and 17th; Tangwan, June 18th and 19th; Beiqiao, June 20th and 21st. 3. Exhibition Hours: First day, 1:00 PM to 6:00 PM; Second day, 7:00 AM to 11:40 AM, 1:00 PM to 3:00 PM. 4. Exhibition Venue: To be found by the local social education institution or district office. 5. Transportation: To be handled by personnel dispatched by the Farmers' Education Center. When necessary, please assist the local education center. 6. Arrangement: To be jointly handled by the Farmers' Education Center and personnel from the local educational institutions or district office. 7. Publicity: A publicity meeting will be held in each location on the first day, inviting local leaders to participate to spread the word and increase efficiency. 8. Custody: During the tour, the Farmers' Education Center is responsible for custody during transportation. Upon arrival at a location, the local social education institution is responsible. If their strength is insufficient, they can send a letter requesting assistance from the local police force. They may also bring a nurse. If there is any shortage or damage, the local social education institution or district office is responsible for compensation. 9. Seeking Opinions: The association will prepare an opinion record and an opinion box to solicit opinions from all sectors on native cloth. 10. Expenses: (1) Food and lodging for the Farmers' Education Center staff (limited to those with badges) are the responsibility of the local social education institution or district office. (2) Transportation costs from location A to location B are borne equally by the Farmers' Education Center and the social education institution in location B. From location B to location C, the transportation costs are borne equally by the Farmers' Education Center and the social education institution in the current location. The association will issue receipts upon receiving funds. (3) Miscellaneous expenses are borne by the local social education institution or district office. 11. Sales: The association may set up a sales department to sell native cloth. Private businesses may also be established with the approval of the association. 12. Supplementary Provisions: If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, they will be negotiated by the Farmers' Education Center and the local social education institution or district office.

Notes from an Ancient Temple (II)(III) 154

The Scholar Who Doesn't Weed His Garden

Twenty-Six

I want to live in the vastness of the sea and sky, which means receiving education in the vastness of the sea and sky. Surely everyone will be happy and get what they want. What more could one ask for? I thought I had obtained Mr. Zhu's magic weapon, but I never expected him to say that I only knew half of it. I had to ask further, "Please tell me, what is the other half?" Mr. Zhu said, "There are three realms of life, and there are three realms of education. What you have proposed is the first realm." How free and happy are the whales in the sea, the cranes in the sky, and the lions in the forest! It is the same happiness when life attains freedom. When education reaches this realm, the classroom becomes paradise, and the children become living deities. But it is clearly a bird in the sky, and someone insists on catching it and putting it in a cage. It is clearly a fish in the sea, and someone insists on catching it and putting it in a bowl. It is clearly a wild beast in the forest, and someone insists on catching it and putting it in a fence. If you were this unfortunate bird, if you were this unfortunate fish, if you were this unfortunate beast, what would you do?" "I don't want to go into the cage. I don't want to go into the bowl. I don't want to go into the fence." "He doesn't care whether you want to or not. He simply captures you and puts you in there, what would you do?" "I will use the power of my small life, I will unite the power of all small lives and fight this person. I will peck through the birdcage, break through the fishbowl, bite through the fence, and flee to the vastness of the sea and sky!" "Or, for example, you are a free lion sleeping in the forest, and suddenly a tiger comes to invade you, what should you do?" "I will fight the tiger to the death!" Mr. Zhu said, "Good, when life encounters an enemy, it must rise up and fight. This is the second realm." I said, "Right! I want freedom! I want to fight!" Mr. Zhu said, "Look at a seed! It is pressed in the soil when it is cold and frozen. You say it is not free when it is pressed by the soil, so you remove the soil. You say it is not free when it is wrapped in the shell, so you peel off the shell. Good, a naked seed is exposed on free land, a hungry bird flies from a dead branch, and swallows it whole! Zhong'er, if this seed wants to sprout, grow, bloom, and bear fruit, you must let it spend some time hidden in the shell, lurking in the ground, slowly absorbing moisture, fertilizer, air, and sunlight to develop its life. This is the third realm."

I was overjoyed and smiled at Mr. Zhu and said, "Sir, you have miscalculated. What I knew was one-third, not half."

American Olympic Track and Field Trials 155

Four Amazing World Records Created

100 Meters, 200 Meters, 110-Meter Hurdles, 220-Yard Low Hurdles

The Tenth Games' Track and Field Championship Belongs to America

The breaking of world records in American track and field has become a daily occurrence. In the past few weeks, George Sipeige, Jim Vance, and Peng Yisimeng have made great contributions in the track and field world, and now Michael F. George Seling, Jackie Shenlei, etc. have successively made great contributions in the track and field world. Previous world records have become past tense, and there is no doubt that future surpassing achievements will continue to come. In short, the heartstrings of American track and field athletes have been stirred by the upcoming opening of the Tenth World Games and have completely entered a state of frenzy. From this point of view, it is difficult for other countries to compete with the United States for the track and field championships in the Tenth Games. If the United States fails to win, it would be an abnormal event in the history of world sports.

Four New Records 156

The American Olympic trials were held in Cleveland on the 12th, creating four new world records. The black athlete Michael F. broke two world records in the 100 meters and 200 meters, with a time of 10.2 seconds in the 100 meters and 20.5 seconds (20 1/2 seconds) in the 200 meters. George Seling's 110-yard hurdles time was 14.1 seconds, shortening the old record by 3/10ths of a second. University of West Xia athlete Jack Gilai's 220-yard low hurdles time was 22.7 seconds.

100 Meters, 200 Meters 157

Michael F.'s creation of two new worlds in one day is unprecedented, and the astonishing nature of his achievements can be described as unparalleled in history. His 100-meter time of 10.2 seconds is 1/5th of a second faster than the old record. The old record was set by American sprint pioneer Pat Ducques in April 23rd, 1921. The 200-meter record of 20.5 seconds is also 1/10th of a second faster than the old record. Rocks' world record set on May 1st, 1926 has now been surpassed by Michael F. However, Michael F.'s start was not perfect, but his finishing skills were excellent, like a storm's speed, and he was able to achieve great success. Michael F. has been very enthusiastic about sports from elementary school to university, and his body is very strong, with a height of 5 feet 11 inches and a weight of 180 pounds, which is rare among athletes.

110-Yard Hurdles 158

George Seling's hurdles are also very impressive. He broke the old record by 3/10ths of a second. This old record was produced as early as 12 years ago, created by Canada's Thompson on May 29th, 1920. Seling is 22 years old this year, 6 feet 1.5 inches tall, and weighs 155 pounds. He is a new hero. In the 70-yard race in the Ten Giants Games, anyone was more than 10 yards behind him. His 220-yard low hurdles also have an excellent record of 20.4 seconds.

220-Yard Low Hurdles 159

Jack Gilai's 220-yard low hurdles shortened the old record by 3/10ths of a second. Bruggan's record set on May 17th, 1924 was 23 seconds. Jack is a student at the University of West Xia and has participated in all-American university competitions and is the hurdles champion of the Western Games. His 50-yard hurdles time is 6.2 seconds.

The details of the situation and Lin's remarks are recorded below:

Persuading Chen to Stay 　Chairman Lin drove out as early as 7:00 AM yesterday morning, arriving at 75 Shanzhong Road at 8:00 AM to visit Minister of Transportation Chen Mingshu, urging him to immediately dismiss his resignation intentions and encouraging him to take on difficult tasks. It is reported that Chen's attitude has softened somewhat due to Chairman Lin's sincere persuasion. If he can take some time to rest fully, he can return to Beijing to resume his duties. Chen and Cai Visit Lin 　Minister of Transportation Chen Mingshu, accompanied by Cai Tingkai, commander of the 19th Route Army, went to Lin's private residence on Jin Shenfu Road at about 2:00 PM to pay their respects. Lin extended his utmost regards to Commander Cai.

Lin's Remarks 　Lin returned to his residence at 12:30 PM, and reporters from various newspapers visited him at this time. He was graciously received and made the following remarks: (Reporter asked) Chairman, you visited Minister Chen today. Has Minister Chen's intention to resign been dismissed? (Answer) Minister Chen's intention to resign can now be dismissed, but because he is too tired, he still needs to rest in Shanghai for a while. However, the date when he can go to Beijing to take up his duties is still uncertain. (Question) Has the Chairman met Minister Song? (Answer) I have not met him yet. I plan to visit and express my regards. (Question) What are the Chairman's views on the issue of the resumption of diplomatic relations between China and Russia? (Answer) This matter is currently under study and consideration by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and a complete plan is being formulated. (Question) Does the Chairman have any opinions on suppressing the communists? (Answer) Currently, not only are the communist bandits rampant, but the bandits are also spreading, so it is urgent to find ways to eliminate them, to stabilize the region and ensure the livelihood of the people. The responsibility should be handled by the military committee to thoroughly suppress them, in order to achieve a permanent solution. (Question) The entire committee of Jiangsu Province recently submitted a general resignation. What does the Chairman think? (Answer) Because I passed through Beijing in a hurry, I have not seen a detailed report. I only saw a general outline in yesterday's newspaper, so I am not yet able to express an opinion. (Question) What is the latest situation in Guangdong? (Answer) It is not as serious as reported. I believe that with Mr. Hu Zhantang mediating, it should not escalate. (Question) When will the Chairman return to Beijing? (Answer) If it rains, I will stay a few more days.

Visit to Sun Did Not Materialize 　Chairman Lin went to visit Sun Ke at Moliai Road at 4:30 PM in the afternoon. He was received by Sun's secretary, Qu Dingxin. Chairman Lin entered the reception room, and Qu reported that Sun had suddenly caught a cold after dinner last night, with dizziness. He was treated by a German doctor in the afternoon and has gradually recovered. After notification, Mr. Sun originally intended to meet with Lin. Chairman Lin, fearing that Sun would be overworked, arranged to meet again another day, and then resigned from Sun's residence and returned to his own.

Since the establishment of the Saito Cabinet in Japan, its aggression against China has become more urgent. Japan's various foreign propaganda are only for domestic purposes. Resumption of Diplomatic Relations Between China and Russia 　(Question) The Northeast customs duties have been withheld.

As for the restoration of diplomatic relations between China and Russia, Russia has always had this hope. This should not be a problem. It is rumored that after the restoration of diplomatic relations between China and Russia, Chen Youren will be sent to Russia as an envoy. I am completely unaware of this. I (Guo himself) am unwilling to express my opinion on the advantages and disadvantages of restoring diplomatic relations. This matter is being carefully considered by the central government and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs beforehand. The date of my trip to England is undecided.

At that time, when asked by reporters, he issued a statement, which was published in various newspapers on April 15, stating "A free city sacrifices sovereignty, and anyone with a conscience will be deeply saddened." He did not believe that discerning people would believe it, and he had solemnly denied it, so he ignored it. As for the recent rumors in small newspapers, they may have come from Japanese newspapers. Whether he loves his country, although he cannot cut open his heart to show the people of the country, but based on his usual principles and actions, as well as his participation in various affairs after the Shanghai Incident, he believes that he will be recognized by patriotic compatriots. Public Letter from the Taicang War Zone Committee 173

Sent to Various Associations, Bureaus, Etc.

Tang Wenzhi, President of the Taicang Branch of the Jiangsu War Zone Relief Committee, Yao Ren, Vice President, Gu Gongliang, etc., yesterday sent letters to the Jiangsu War Zone Relief Committee, the Shanghai Standing Committee of the Jiangsu War Zone Relief Committee, the Jiading and Baoshan Branches of the Jiangsu War Zone Relief Committee, the Taicang County Magistrate, the Taicang County Party Headquarters, and other bureaus and associations, stating, We hereby respectfully inform you that the war zone relief affairs shall be in accordance with the provisions of Article 13 of the Jiangsu War Zone Relief Committee Ordinance, which was resolved and implemented by the Jiangsu Provincial Government, and a branch shall be established in Taicang. Before the promulgation of the ordinance, there was an organization of the Taicang War Disaster Relief Association. Now, after a meeting, it has been decided that the unfinished matters handled by the War Disaster Relief Association shall be completed later, and the branch shall be reorganized in accordance with the regulations to conform to the system. The name shall be changed to the Taicang Branch of the Jiangsu War Zone Relief Committee, and Wenzhi shall be appointed as the President, and Yao Ren and Gongliang shall be appointed as the Vice Presidents. A new seal will be published and used immediately. We hereby inform you, and we hope that you will check and acknowledge it.

Situation of the Shengjing Ship Salvage 180

The Taikoo Company's Shengjing ship hit a reef at Qingming Island in Weihaiwei, and the passengers were rescued, as recorded in yesterday's newspaper. Following are the additional details from yesterday:

Shengjing Set into Reef Stone 　The Shengjing ship encountered fog and hit a reef. The bow of the ship hit into the reef stone, and two large holes have been formed. The reef stone is set inside the bow of the ship, and the seawater entering the bow cabin has reached 11 and a half feet. The ship's body has become a symbol of front sinking and rear rising, and it cannot reverse. Except when the tide rises and floats the ship, it is impossible to get it out.

Cargo Has Been Unloaded First 　The ship is loaded with 3,000 to 4,000 pieces of cargo, and there are also many head foreign cloth pieces. Those loaded in the head cabin have been completely immersed in the water. The middle and rear cabins have not been affected. Each passenger family went to inquire, and the company has decided to clear all the cargo. The Fengtian ship has been dispatched from Tanggu and is currently unloading. It is to be expected that after the cargo is unloaded, the ship will be lighter and easier to float.

Engineers Go to Inspect 　The cost and layout of the ship must be worth one million yuan. The Shanghai branch decided on a rescue plan yesterday, and planned to first find a way to get the reef stone that was set in to escape, and then use water boards and wooden boards for temporary repairs, but the procedure was tedious. Therefore, the Shanghai branch invited two engineers from the Jiangnan Shipyard, and the Shanghai branch appointed staff and applied equipment, etc., and released the Ningbo ship yesterday morning to sail to Qingming Island to try to salvage and rescue it.

Japanese Salvage Ship Has Arrived 　After the accident on the Shengjing, the bank telegraphed the Japanese Salvage Company to send a ship to rescue it. The Japanese Salvage Ship Company dispatched a salvage work ship near Dalian Bay, which arrived yesterday. Divers are now being sent into the seabed to inspect the situation of the grounding reef. However, according to news from the bank yesterday, the Shengjing ship is expected to be rescued no matter what, but the weather was still good yesterday morning, which was conducive to work, but there were winds and waves in the afternoon, which hindered the salvage work.

All Passengers Escaped Safely 　A total of 350 passengers and crew members on board, after the British destroyer Warren and the naval tugboat went to rescue them, the company continued to receive a telegram yesterday afternoon that all the crew members and passengers on board had been completely rescued and sent to Weihaiwei by 9:00 AM on the 14th. Captain Li Dexu is still on board, directing rescue and other affairs.

A Large Number of Warships Protect 　In addition to sending two destroyers to assist in the rescue, the British Navy on Liugong Island dispatched three or four more destroyers to Qingming Island yesterday, anchoring on the left and right of the Shengjing ship to prevent pirates from looting.

Japan has designated Shanghai as a plague-stricken port, and passengers going east from this port have already implemented stool examinations. However, among the passengers disembarking from the Dalian Steamship Company's Tianjin Maru, which came to Shanghai from Tianjin, there were also people suffering from the plague. When the ship arrived in Qingdao, it was banned from entry by the local customs and the ship was moved outside the port. Disinfection was carried out inside the ship, and the infected passengers were sent to the plague hospital for isolation. The date of the Tianjin Maru's arrival in Shanghai was therefore delayed by two days.

The Nine-Road Business Federation on Aiwunyi Road issued a declaration yesterday, saying that the opium monopoly cannot be implemented in our country, and the national government entrusted by public opinion has no room to argue. Telephone Workers' Strike 186

Workers Submit Protest Letter Yesterday

The strike of workers at the concession telephone company entered its eighth day yesterday. The strike committee submitted a protest letter to the company, demanding a response within twenty-four hours. The details are as follows:

Submitting the Protest: At 2:00 PM yesterday, representatives Chen Yaozu, Xu Shize, Ye Yilong, and others, along with representatives from various departments, went to the New Central Bank on Fujian Road to submit a protest letter to the company. They were received by engineer Wilson. The representatives stated that the company had repeatedly and unjustifiably rejected the workers' demands, leading to the strike and disrupting public utilities, for which the company should be held responsible. Furthermore, the company's notice slandered all employees and dismissed twelve workers from the northern branch. This extreme oppression of workers could lead to unforeseen consequences in the future. The strike committee, representing over three thousand employees, issued a serious warning to the company, demanding a written response within twenty-four hours of the protest letter's arrival. The company has agreed to respond today.

Strike Committee Announcement: The Youth Workers' Department of the strike committee announced yesterday: "The strike is now at a critical stage. All our young workers must resolutely fight. Each department should convene a meeting of young workers tonight to (1) discuss the organization of youth worker pickets and propaganda teams, (2) discuss the unique suffering and demands of youth workers, and (3) each department must send one representative to a meeting at 11:00 AM on the 15th to discuss these issues."

Strike Tribunal: In order to deal with those who violate strike discipline, the strike committee established a strike tribunal yesterday, appointing a chief judge to be designated by the strike committee's presidium, and seven judges, one each from the Fujian Road, Min'er Road, Jiangxi Road, Metterhurst Road, and Haining Road branches, as well as the picket department and the youth workers' department. Strike regulations have also been promulgated.

According to the Navigation Administration, the Hong Kong government previously restricted the entry of Chinese vessels captained by foreign captains because China had not joined the International Convention for the Safety of Life at Sea. The Birth of Chinese Military Music 192

Historically, Chinese music before the Three Dynasties, although divided into Shao music and Wu music, both belonged to the realm of civil virtue. Purely martial military music originated with the Dayu music of the Eastern Han Dynasty, reaching its peak in the Tang Dynasty, and gradually declining after the Song Dynasty. Although the late Qing Dynasty had types such as triumphant music and gong and drum music, they were not very developed. In the mid-Guangxu period, Western military music entered China, and its influence grew daily. Today, national and social institutions, as well as groups, all use Western music, which has a significant impact on national identity. Recently, there has been a growing call for traditional Chinese music, but it has remained within the cultural sphere. Therefore, the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce has initiated a project to revive ancient military music, led by Zheng Jinwen of the Datong Music Society. A small team (60 people) will be formed first, with instruments divided into (wind), (string), (plucked), and (percussion) sections, totaling more than 30 types, manufactured using modern methods, with the standards being large volume, portability, and ease of carrying. The musical scores will be selected from appropriate ancient war songs. The team members will be composed of Boy Scouts from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and training will begin soon. It is also reported that the Datong Music Society's large orchestra will be recruiting 20 more musicians to expand its size. Those with basic musical knowledge can register at No. 36 Songshan Road at the society's office.

The meeting adjourned at 6:30 PM.

Unexpected Twist in Pudong Rent Reduction 194

Since being approved by the Municipal Rent Reduction Movement Committee, the Pudong District Rent Reduction Movement Committee immediately petitioned the Municipal Party Headquarters, the Municipal Government, and the Five District Party Headquarters to reduce rents. Upon receiving the petition, the Five District Party Headquarters went to the Pudong Chamber of Commerce to discuss rent reduction measures in order to find an appropriate solution. Yesterday (14th), the Pudong Rent Reduction Committee suddenly received a notice from the Third District Public Security Bureau, and dispatched a representative to the bureau. Section Chief Niu of the Third District Public Security Bureau expressed the following opinions to the representative: (1) Pudong is not a war zone and should not reduce rents; (2) Both the Rent Reduction Committee and the Tenants' Union are among the prohibited organizations; (3) Land prices in Shanghai have increased, so there is only reason to increase rents, not reduce them; (4) The committee must stop its work immediately; (5) The seals used should be confiscated, but to save face, the matter will not be pursued further. It is reported that the Rent Reduction Committee believes that the rent reduction movement is intended to relieve the suffering of the common people and involves no illegal activities, so they are extremely indignant that Section Chief Niu would make such statements. They have immediately submitted a report to the Party and government organs and the General Committee for instructions. They will continue their work until they receive orders from the Municipal Party Headquarters, the Municipal Government, the Five District Party Headquarters, and the Municipal Rent Reduction General Committee.

Zhabei Public Bus 200

Route 3 Restored to Original Condition

The Zhabei Chinese Public Bus Company, in order to restore its operations, is striving to resume business. Route 1, which runs from the Jishan Road intersection directly to Jiangwan, is temporarily suspended due to the bombing of the Yokohama Road Bridge, which has not yet been repaired. Route 3, which runs from the Jishan Road intersection to Zhenru, resumed operations on June 1st and is running as usual. However, because the iron barriers at the Baoshan Road intersection were removed and the Qiujiang Road surface was not repaired, the company was granted permission by the Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities to temporarily change the route, starting from the North Station Jielu, along Xinmin Road, Datong Road, and Jiaotong Road, directly to Zhenru. Now that the Public Concession has announced the lifting of martial law on the 13th, and the barbed wire at the Baoshan Road intersection has been removed on the same day, North Henan Road is now directly connected to Baoshan Road. Therefore, the company's Route 3 will also restore its previous route from the 14th, starting from the Baoshan Road intersection, along Qiujiang Road, Gonghe Xin Road, and Jiaotong Road, directly to Zhenru. The fare schedule remains the same. Station 2 was originally the South Seas Business Association, but because that station was too short, it was changed to Song Park Road. Station 10 was changed to Xiaochangmiao. The fare for the entire route remains the same.

Bureau of Social Affairs 201

Promoting the New System of Weights and Measures

The Public Concession will also implement it

The new system of weights and measures in this city, after being promoted by the Bureau of Social Affairs, has recently become increasingly effective. The Chinese area has been fully implemented, and the French Concession has also been implemented. The Public Concession has not yet been implemented. The Bureau of Social Affairs is planning to thoroughly promote the system of weights and measures. The situation of trial implementation of weights and measures in each district is recorded below:

Nanshi District: Nanshi District was the earliest district to implement weights and measures and has now fully implemented it and has been re-examined four or five times. However, some stores still use old-fashioned weights and measures due to habit, making it impossible to unify the new system. The Municipal Weights and Measures Verification Office is planning to conduct another re-examination.

Zhabei District: The promotion of the new system of weights and measures in Zhabei was also quite early, so now all stores and vegetable markets use the new system of weights and measures. After the Shanghai War, many residents still used old measures. A re-examination is also planned.

French Concession: The promotion of the new system of weights and measures in the French Concession, after several contacts with the French authorities by the Bureau of Social Affairs, has now been implemented. However, it has not been implemented for long, so it is not yet fully unified. The Bureau of Social Affairs plans to increase re-examination to promote the unification of weights and measures. The Public Concession has not yet implemented the new system. The Bureau of Social Affairs is in contact with the Concession authorities and it is expected to be implemented soon.

Extortion Case Against Electrical Factory Owner 204

Southern Bandit Sentenced to Two Years

Yu Shengsan from Hunan and Li Zicai from Wuxi, for writing threatening letters from May 21st to the first of this month, and delivering them to Hu Yueshan, the local owner of the Jintai Electrical Factory at No. 210 Grant Road, Yangshupu, demanding 10,000 dollars, signed "Southeast Self-Defense Army's Rear Service Preparation Office," and arranging a meeting near the Xietu Road bridge in the French Concession, with violent language, were reported to the

Yangshupu Police Station. The police station dispatched Chinese detectives Shen Wanzhou, Shan Zhaoxian, and Guo Jingbang, along with Qian Wancai, the representative of Hu, to the agreed location. They first captured Yu, who confessed that Li Zicai was hiding at the Kaitai Hotel at No. 12 Beihai Road. The detectives went secretly and captured Li. They were taken to the First Special District Court for interrogation. Yesterday morning, judge Qiao Wanxuan continued the interrogation in the first division. The police station's lawyer Zhang Tianyin stated that the Kaitai Hotel's cashier and tea server had brought the registration book for Li Zicai's room to the court, and the registered name was Li Zong, Li Zicai's alias. He requested an inquiry. According to Rong Jinbao, the cashier of the Kaitai Hotel, and Chen Wenbin, the tea server, Li Zhisui, Li Zhisui, had been living in the hotel for more than a month, and Yu Shengsan had also stayed there for two or three nights. They knew each other and played mahjong several times, but they did not know about the threatening letter. The registration book was presented to the court. The two defendants denied the charges, claiming that they were committed by a certain Jia who was at large, overturning their confession to the police station. Judge Qiao instructed the police station's lawyer Zhang and the defendants' attorney to begin the debate. Lawyer Zhang stated that the two defendants had fully admitted to the police station that they had jointly discussed and carried out the act, and the confession was clear and without coercion. Therefore, he requested the court to impose a severe sentence according to law. Judge Qiao then sentenced Yu Shengsan and Li Zicai to two years in prison each for the crime of joint extortion. The number of days of detention before the judgment was determined will be credited at a rate of two days to one day of imprisonment. The threatening letter was confiscated.
