Commentary

Parting in Joy 271

— Buddha

The other day, in the alley where I live, two Jiangbei children were fighting. One was stronger, the other weaker. The weaker child was beaten by the stronger child, his head was bleeding, and he cried loudly. The stronger child, fearing that bystanders would take up the cause, immediately comforted him with kind words and bought a piece of candy from a candy vendor, putting it in the weaker child’s mouth. The weaker child, his head still bleeding, wiped his hands, turned from sorrow to joy, and reconciled with the other child as if nothing had happened. In the end, both children parted in joy.

After the Shu Kingdom fell, Liu Shan moved his entire family to Luoyang. The Wei court enfeoffed him as the Duke of Anle. One day, at a banquet, the Wei court had Shu performers perform. Everyone else felt sorrowful, but Liu Shan smiled as if nothing had happened. Zhao said to Jia Chong, "This man is so devoid of emotion that even if Zhuge Liang were alive, he could not have supported him for long." He then asked Liu Shan, "Do you miss Shu?" Liu Shan replied, "I am happy here and do not miss Shu." In the end, they also parted in joy.

I saw a scene of parting in joy in my alley and another in history. It made me feel uneasy. According to a newspaper report yesterday, Japanese Ambassador Shigemitsu and Consul-General Murai, in view of the signing of the Shanghai Armistice Agreement, urgently sought to promote friendship between China and Japan. They hosted a banquet at Yue Nai’s house at 7 PM last night, inviting two important Chinese diplomatic officials, Guo Taiqi and Jiang Zuobin, to show their solidarity. During the banquet, they conversed happily, and discussions were lively. They parted in joy at 9 PM.

So that is what parting in joy is! Alas!

Literature

Four Elegies for the Northeast 272

— Dream Box Master

With the signing of the ceasefire agreement, the Shanghai Incident has come to an end, but half of the Northeast remains in enemy hands. The government has no intention of recovering it, and the people of Shanghai are gradually forgetting it. Therefore, I have collected old news and written these four elegies for the Northeast to alert the people of the nation, lest I be accused of lamenting yesterday’s news.

Elegy for Shenyang 273

In Shenyang city, there were one hundred thousand soldiers,

Camps were stationed south and north of the city.

At midnight, the bandits came and all the soldiers fled,

Four days were dark, without a sound of battle.

At dawn, they formed teams to search the wealthy households,

Breaking down doors like wolves, entering like tigers.

Mothers fled with their children, wives sought their husbands,

Our army was far away, in vain they cried out.

The blood and marrow of ten thousand families stained the mud,

They did not care about the scorched fish in the pond.

The treasures of Tianlu, four cabinets of books,

Were all stolen and loaded onto boats back to Penglai.

The majestic arsenal also fell into enemy hands,

Ten years of management, alas, what is the use?

I heard that the Eastern Army was a powerful force,

But why did it turn into a cowardly mouse overnight?

Great generals are not born, heroic men are sad,

The homeland is lost, tears fall like rain.

Do not sing the border city's White Goose Ballad,

The Great Marshal is still enjoying himself on the river.

Elegy for Changchun 274

Wherever the enemy army goes, the grass bends,

South of Changchun, there are no intact forts.

Surrendering to the enemy is too easy, killing the enemy is too rare,

The isolated city is defended solely by a lone army.

Two hundred and twenty men, none surrendered,

Their survival depends on the city’s survival, their death on its death.

Ten thousand horses press down on the city, and the city seems to move,

The brave soldiers on the city walls surge with energy.

Bathing in blood, they fight without retreat,

One man raises his arm, and a hundred men follow.

They ride their horses and slash into the enemy formation like flying dragons,

Together, they fight to the death to become heroic ghosts.

When they see the enemy, they shave their heads with sharp knives,

They maneuver left and right as they please.

Enemy soldiers who come are all brought to the ground,

Thousands of voices shout to kill the Japanese.

The Japanese are not all killed, more keep coming,

My strength is exhausted, what can I do?

After a day of hard fighting, their lives end together,

The bloody blade is still in their hands, their eyes still wide open.

Is this not my heart, but my integrity?

Science

Manufacturing Methods for Several Daily Necessities 275

— Qing

Rust-Preventative Oil: Iron daily necessities are bright and lubricated when new, making them easy to use. After a while, they easily rust, losing their beauty and becoming unusable. Items such as kitchen knives require special attention to hygiene to prevent the spread of disease. Rust-preventative oil can prevent rust and decay, making it an indispensable item for daily use. The raw materials include 15 parts of resin, 500 parts of mica powder, 250 parts of lard, 45 parts of beeswax, and 45 parts each of olive oil and turpentine. The method involves placing the resin, lard, olive oil, and beeswax in an iron pot, melting them over low heat, and mixing well. Then, add the mica powder and remove from heat. Finally, add the turpentine and mix well.

Smelling Salts: The use of smelling salts is extremely common. They can be used to prevent epidemics and remove odors in both cities and villages. Residents of this city should have them on hand, as epidemics can easily occur after war. During the hot summer months, they are especially needed. The method involves using equal parts of charcoal, quicklime, and crude alum. Grind each of the three materials separately and place them in a glass bottle. When you want to use them, take a small amount of the powder, mix it with clean water, and sprinkle it in the corners of the room. This can prevent plagues and remove odors, and it is much cheaper than buying them on the market.

Silvered Glass: Silvered glass has many uses and is often sold in stores. The method involves using ammonia water, silver nitrate, and glucose in a ratio of 2:4:1, along with appropriate amounts of alcohol and clean water. Dissolve 6 parts each of ammonia water, silver nitrate, and alcohol water (i.e., six times the amount of glucose used) into a liquid, then filter to clarify it. Separately, dissolve 1 part each of glucose and alcohol water into a liquid. Mix this liquid with the previous liquid. Then, wash a glass object and immerse it in the successfully mixed liquid. After two or three days, it will turn into silvered glass.

Fiction

Wedding Night 276

— Ang Lian

A bustling wedding day had passed.

It was about midnight. G's mother and aunts sent him into the bridal chamber. The anxiety that had plagued him all day finally disappeared, thinking that from now on, it would be "a hundred years of harmony."

"G, you can get up a little later tomorrow. You look tired today," G's mother said gently as she stepped out the door.

G only responded with a "hmm." His head was heavy and throbbing, feeling like a homeless wandering soul. He saw the bride sitting on the edge of the bed adjusting her clothes, and a sudden thought surged into his heart, causing him to shiver.

"It's over!" he blurted out.

The bride was a little bewildered. She looked up and saw his face as if covered with frost, his eyes wide and frightening, staring at her as if possessed. She felt uneasy, unable to guess why he showed such grief. The wedding night should be filled with curiosity and sweetness.

Outside the window, a light rain began to fall, making her feel even more unhappy. Suddenly, she heard a sob coming from the groom who was slumped on the table. The sorrowful weeping, in the dead of night, faintly resembled the pain of a wounded beast. She had never heard a man cry so terribly, and she shivered slightly.

"This is a very bad omen!" she thought.

Two o'clock had passed. The crying had stopped, but she was still waiting for him on the edge of the bed, feeling impatient and very tired. She began to feel hatred towards him. After his crying stopped, she sat motionless like a stone statue, afraid to disturb him. She was shy, and she wondered how a country girl could easily be the first to speak to him. But he was a man, wasn't he being unreasonable? A terrible image enveloped her heart. She felt like an abandoned woman.

"Maybe he doesn't think I'm pretty, so he..." she worried, thinking over and over. She felt so sleepy that she could no longer bear to wait.

Three o'clock, four o'clock... had passed. The night dragged on.

When she woke up, she rubbed her sleepy eyes and felt around her. Was anyone there? No? The sun was shining in through the window. The chair was empty. G had left sometime.

While she was washing up, her mother-in-law brought a letter, her face full of tears, and said, "He's gone! G ran away last night!" Her mother-in-law sobbed.

"..." The bride couldn't speak. She realized that the bad omen had come true. It seemed that her fate was predetermined. She was an abandoned woman. But who had abandoned her? Was it G, or her parents? Her mind was confused.

G's father rushed in and opened G's letter to read.

"Goodbye! My parents! I would rather sacrifice my studies, I would rather not have the family provide for my life, I would rather suffer in the dark society, than submit to the inhumane feudal etiquette and the iron heel of the all-evil money of this society, to marry a woman I do not know and do not love. Goodbye, forgive me for sullying your family's 'good reputation.' Your son, G."

"Etiquette..." The bride seemed to hear these two new words. She felt a wave of dizziness and fell down...

Social Issues

After Unemployment 277

— Yi Xue

Because his wife was sick, he asked for a few extra days off from his work. The high-nosed boss put on the face of a capitalist and fired him.

A year ago, introduced by a good classmate, he passed the exam and entered this high-nosed foreigner's firm. He brought his newlywed wife from the countryside and rented a small room. Although the salary at the firm was small, they lived frugally. The life of a husband and wife could be maintained. Half a year later, a son was born. They loved this crystallization of love even more. Every day he saved on transportation costs to buy nutritious food for his son.

This happiness amidst hardship was enough to make them content. His wife! Perhaps due to overwork, or perhaps because the small room in the three-story alley building built by capitalists had too polluted air, she contracted a seasonal epidemic. In that small room, he had to protect his son from coming into contact with the patient, and he also had to take care of his wife. Shanghai doctors who didn't gouge were not famous doctors. A small clerk in a foreign firm was of course unable to cope. Their finances became panicked. At first, they could still pawn things to get by. After a week, the high-nosed boss sent him a letter because he had taken too much leave, firing him. In his confused state of mind, he didn't even think about what he would do in the future. The most important thing was how to get through the present. He had no choice but to borrow from closer relatives. As the saying goes, "Few give charcoal in the snow, old faces have no shame in adding flowers to brocade." Seeing his poor appearance, they didn't even offer ordinary perfunctory words, sending him away coldly.

He walked forward aimlessly, wandering to the Huangpu River. Looking at the rolling river, he lamented how many heroes and heroines were buried in it. He himself had a bellyful of talent, but he couldn't even support his wife and son. He was just thinking of lightly jumping in, which would end all his troubles, but a shocking wooden sign from the Social Bureau caught his eye: "You must not die, turn back!" He shook his head and wanted to run home quickly. He seemed to hear someone say to him, "Your wife is sick, your son is hungry, if you don't die, what will you do!"

A burst of waves suddenly arose in the still river, circles of waves slowly enlarging to infinity.

Automobile News

Commentary

An Overview of the New Ford 282

13 Million Visitors

Since its debut, the new Ford car has shone brightly in the automotive world. In addition to announcing the various reforms and excellent features of the new car to the world, the factory has also distributed sample cars to dealers, displaying them widely in major cities to attract attention. According to the American Automotive Business News, since Ford dealers displayed the new car models in their showrooms, tens of thousands of people have visited and inspected the new cars daily. As of recently, the total number of visitors has reached as many as 13 million. Furthermore, according to Mr. Crow, the Chinese manager of Ford, 300,000 units of the new Ford V8 car displayed in various places were immediately ordered by visitors, which shows that the excellent quality of the new car has deeply impressed people. An independent automotive publication praised the new car as representing the progress and success of Ford's 29 years of car-making experience, and stated that its innovations and improvements are entirely based on its historical practice and the integration of various strengths.

Before the emergence of the Ford V8 and four-cylinder new cars, the factory had been preparing and operating for several months. It employed over 100,000 workers to manufacture the new cars. According to the "Automobile Daily," Ford's eagerness to launch the new cars was due to the personal encouragement of President Hoover, who deeply knew that the increase in car sales could actually make the recovery of the United States' prosperity easier. According to Ford himself, the V8 new car he manufactured has extremely sufficient horsepower, but its management is simple and easy, just like the two characteristics of its speed and power. As for its pricing, it is based on the principle that both buyers and sellers get their fair share. Ford also said that he did not care about the cost of manufacturing. If he had to consider it, the price would inevitably increase accordingly. However, in this economic downturn, how could the selling price be increased again? Therefore, time and money are not taken into account. His responsibility is only to find ways to allow workers to have work to do as soon as possible.

In addition to expressing the above views, Ford also said that in addition to the V8 new car with 65 horsepower, Ford also makes a four-cylinder car with 50 horsepower. Cars with various cylinder numbers have 14 different body styles. These two four-cylinder and eight-cylinder cars have no significant differences other than the structure of the engine. The body and frame are the same, but their prices are different. Because the V8 car will be listed among low-priced cars, the price of the four-cylinder car is even cheaper than the V8 car. Ford said that the reason why the company does this is to serve the public who use cars, and to provide buyers with cheap and good cars in the autumn of economic instability.

The characteristics of the new car cannot be fully described for a while. To list the most obvious ones, there is the silent simultaneous action gear lever, silent gears, rubber-coated engine, carbonized silencer, automatic spark management, a bulkhead pump that inputs fuel from the rear fuel tank to the engine. In addition, there are flexible and bendable upper arm springs, new rear springs, automatic self-adjusting Hale double-action hydraulic shock absorbers, large four-wheel brakes, and new electric forged steel spoke wheels with large hubs and hubcaps and large wheel rims. Rubber is used as insulation between the frame and the gears, so that the movement of the springs and links does not affect the body. Rubber is also embedded between the body and the frame.

The style of the body from the V-shaped radiator to the rear end is exceptionally fresh and beautiful. The long head is streamlined and has stainless steel straight lines. The windshield has inclined safety glass. The roof is rounded. Other features such as the protruding headlights, the front fender guard, and the low and long footboard are all coordinated and aesthetically pleasing with the whole body. The interior of the carriage is very spacious. The decoration is also extremely luxurious. The seats are new and quite comfortable. The driver's seat can be adjusted in all sedans. There is a ventilation device on the roof. The instrument panel is oval and lined with stainless steel sheets. All sedans have folding sun visors.

Ford's V-shaped engine has an angle of 90 degrees and has a power of 30 horsepower, a braking force of 65 horsepower, and 3,400 revolutions per minute. The pistons are made of aluminum alloy and have three ring loops. The lower one is used for oil control. The cylinder head and crankcase are cast together, making the structure very strong. The new valve tail is shaped like a bamboo mat and is operated by a crankshaft. The engine does not use intermediate gears. Spark management is automatic. The lubrication of the crankcase and crankpins is caused by pressure. The lubrication of the pistons and valves uses the splash method. The fan in the cooling system is designed as an airplane dark wheel and has an off-center water pump and a wide-gas heat dissipation method. Therefore, no matter how the car travels, it can maintain its cooling effect.

Automobile Driving Knowledge 283

— Shi Weilie

Due to the arrival of summer, the wheel tracks of cars on the road are denser than at other times. The occurrence of tragedies is also much higher than at other times. In view of the occurrence of various unfortunate incidents in the past, the Motor Vehicle Department of the Public Works Bureau has newly promulgated several driving tips. Those who like to sit in cars for a ride, that is, all those who drive cars, please pay attention to the new suggestions below and use them as a warning for driving.

(1) Speed. Driving fast can be said to be the cause of accidents, but it is not the main culprit. The most important thing is to match the speed with the environment. Often, at the same speed, there is a distinction between stable and dangerous due to different situations. Therefore, those who like to drive fast must always pay attention to everything around them.

(2) Hand Signals. When you raise your hand to signal, you must be consistent in mind and action. If your hand signals are clear and accurate, then no matter when stopping, turning, or driving onto another intersection, there will never be an unfortunate incident.

(3) Overtaking. If you do not have sufficient time or complete certainty, do not cross your car forward when vehicles are crowded on an intersection.

(4) Safe Distance. The car in front of you may suddenly stop. You must always maintain a considerable distance to avoid the misfortune of a collision.

(5) Sudden Stops. Except in cases of absolute necessity, do not suddenly stop your vehicle. You must remember that there are other vehicles following behind you.

(6) On the Tracks. Although there are gates and warning signs on the railway tracks, or pipe workers guarding them, you must pay attention yourself and treat yourself as a patrol officer.

(7) Traffic Signals (Traffic Lights, etc.). Traffic signals are set up for your safety. If you destroy traffic signals for a very short time, then the unfortunate fact is the result.

(8) New Routes. When driving on roads that you do not often visit, you must always pay attention. Unexpected disturbances may hit you unexpectedly.

News

Overview of Henan Province Highways 284

Black Fox

Transportation is essential for enlightening the people and developing industry, and highways are especially a shortcut to facilitate transportation and achieve twice the result with half the effort. Henan Province is adjacent to Hebei, Shandong, Jiangsu, Anhui, Hubei, Shaanxi, and Shanxi, seven provinces. It is the center of culture and industry in our country. Although there is now the Longhai Railway, which connects Jiangsu in the east and Shaanxi in the west, and the Pinghan Railway, which connects Hebei in the north and Hubei in the south, the western and eastern parts of Henan are still mostly blocked. Therefore, industry is still stagnant, culture remains backward, and bandits cannot be suppressed. To this day, people's lives are becoming increasingly impoverished. Therefore, developing transportation and building provincial highways should be the province's only top priority. The following is an overview of the Henan Provincial Highway Bureau's planned implementation of construction and the status of roads that have already been opened to traffic for reference by those who are enthusiastic about road administration.

Status of Route Work. (1) Kao Deng Line. From the Shandong provincial border, passing through Kaocheng, Lanfeng, Kaifeng, Weishi, Jianchuan, Xuchang, Xiangxian, Yexian, Fangcheng, Nanyang, Dengxian, reaching the Kaohekou of the Hubei provincial border, it is a total of over 920 li in length. It is crucial to connect the transportation of Shandong, Henan, and Hubei provinces. It should be completed in the first phase of construction. Passing through the old Yellow River course, the Jialu River, the Shuangji River, the Ying River, the Ru River, the Rufen River, the Feng River, the Zhan River, the Hun River, the Sanli River, the Mazi River, the Yanshanpu River, the Pan River, the Zhao River, the Bai River, the Liao River, the Tuan River, the Xiajia River, and other rivers, there are no formal bridges. In addition to the original 29 bridges, which should be usable, another 23 solid bridges should be added. A total of 68 culverts should be added and repaired along the entire line, laying 57 cement water pipes. The earthwork volume is 993,100 cubic meters. (2) An Shang Line. From the Hebei provincial border, passing through Fenglezhen, Anyang, Tangyin, Junxian, Daokou, Fengqiu, Kaifeng, Chenliu, Qixian, Taikang, Huaiyang, Xiangcheng, Xincai, Huangchuan, Shangcheng, reaching the Hubei provincial border, the entire line is over 1,280 li in length. In the first phase, the An Shang section will be constructed first. This section is the only main line in southeastern Henan Province, from Kaifeng to the Hubei provincial border, with a total length of over 950 li. Extremely solid large bridges will be built across the Shahe, Banghe, Bailu River, and Quhe rivers to facilitate traffic. There are a total of 164 bridges and culverts of various sizes on the entire road, laying 126 water pipes. The earthwork volume is 1,577,200 cubic meters. (3) Shan San Line. From the Shanxi provincial border, passing through Shaanxian, Lushi, Jingziguan (Shaanxi provincial border), Zhechuan, Dengxian, Xinye, Tongbai, Xinyang, Luoshan, Huangchuan, Gushi, reaching Sanhejian, Anhui Province
